The initial \"Committee on Bible Translation\" consisted of E. Leslie Carlson, Edmund Clowney, Ralph Earle, Jr., Burton L. Goddard, R. Laird Harris, Earl S. Kalland, Kenneth Kantzer, Robert H. The range of those participating included many different denominations such as Anglicans, Assemblies of God, Baptist, Christian Reformed, Lutheran and Presbyterian.\r\n\r\nThe NIV is a balance between word-for-word and thought-for-thought or literal and phrase by phrase translations.\r\n\r\nRecent archaeological and linguistic discoveries helped in understanding passages that have traditionally been difficult to translate.
